*Mahesh Bhosale,Naresh Kumar Devulapally,Abdul Wasi,Chau Pham,Vishnu Suresh Lokhande,David Doermann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文从“分数平滑性导致扩散模型幻觉”这一经验假设出发，给出密度与Lipschitz视角的理论刻画，并提出方差引导的分数调制(VSM)在采样时控制分数雅可比，从而降低幻觉概率。在合成与真实数据上可将幻觉降低约25%，且保持保真度与多样性，并发布两套极端语义变化的评测基准与代码数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型尽管在多模态生成中表现卓越，但会产生与真实数据分布不一致的幻觉样本，影响可靠性。现有对“分数过度平滑”原因的理解多为经验性，需要更严谨的理论与有效的实用缓解策略及可重复评测基准。

Method: 1) 从密度估计角度将幻觉质量与学习到的分数函数的平滑性联系起来，并将幻觉概率质量与分数的Lipschitz常数建立形式化关联；2) 提出Variance-Guided Score Modulation (VSM)：在采样过程中依据噪声/方差调节分数的雅可比以降低平滑性，使估计分数更贴近真实分数；3) 构建两套具有极端语义变化的数据集作为系统化幻觉评测基准。

Result: 在合成与真实数据集上，VSM可将幻觉率最多降低约25%，同时基本不损失图像保真度与多样性；实验验证了分数平滑性与幻觉之间的经验性假设，并给出了密度与Lipschitz视角的一致证据。

Conclusion: 控制分数函数的平滑性（通过VSM调制分数雅可比）是降低扩散模型幻觉的有效、可解释且通用的途径；提出的理论联系与基准为更可靠的扩散式图像生成提供了原则化方向。

Abstract: Diffusion models have emerged as the backbone of modern generative AI, powering advances in vision, language, audio and other modalities. Despite their success, they suffer from hallucinations, implausible samples that lie outside the support of true data distribution, which degrade reliability and trust. In this work, we first empirically confirm previously proposed hypothesis that score smoothness causes hallucinations in Image Generation diffusion models and provide a density-based perspective. We further formalize this notion by linking the hallucinations probability mass to lipschitz constant of the learned score function. Motivated by this, we introduce a Variance-Guided Score Modulation (VSM) strategy that controls the score Jacobian, in turn reducing score smoothness and better approximating the ground truth score that decreases hallucinations. Empirical results on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our approach reduces hallucinations (up to ~25%) while maintaining high fidelity and diversity, providing a principled step toward more reliable diffusion-based image generation. We also propose two benchmark datasets with extreme semantic variation for systematic hallucination evaluation. Code and Datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/bhosalems/VSM.

</details>


### [39] [Non-Learning Low-Light Stereo Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00379)
*Jason Wang,Lucas Nguyen,Hyunseung Eom,Wei Xu,Qi Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种非学习的双目立体匹配框架，利用结点场（FoJ）提取抗噪结构特征构建代价体，并结合边界感知的SGM自适应光滑惩罚，得到在严重噪声下更精确但稀疏的视差图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在严重光子噪声或低照度条件下，传统或学习型立体匹配依赖的细纹理特征易被噪声淹没，导致代价体不可靠、边界被过度平滑，最终视差错误率高。需要一种能够在强噪声下仍稳定利用结构信息、并保护真实视差不连续性的方案。

Method: 1) 引入Field of Junctions（FoJ）表示图像中的粗结构与结点，抑制与噪声难分的细纹理，仅保留稳健的结构线索；2) 基于FoJ构建代价体，使匹配代价更多依赖稳定结构；3) 设计边界感知的半全局匹配（SGM），根据FoJ提供的边界动态调整平滑项惩罚，避免跨越真实不连续处的过度平滑；4) 输出稀疏视差，仅在结构可靠区域给出结果。

Result: 在多项广泛使用的基准数据集上，对未遮挡像素（未掩膜区域），所得稀疏视差图的精度优于多种最新双目算法，尤其在严重噪声条件下表现突出。

Conclusion: 通过以FoJ为核心的结构引导和边界自适应SGM，可在强噪声环境下获得更可靠的（尽管稀疏）视差估计，验证了非学习范式在极端成像条件下的竞争力。

Abstract: We present a non-learning stereo framework for disparity estimation from severely noisy images. Using the Field of Junctions (FoJ), it retains coarse visual features stable under severe noise for cost volume construction while discarding fine textures inseparable from photon noise. The resulting structural information guides boundary-aware Semi-Global Matching (SGM) that dynamically adapts smoothness penalties to preserve true disparity discontinuities. The output is a sparse disparity map more accurate than those of recent stereo algorithms over unmasked pixels on widely-used benchmark datasets.

</details>


### [40] [SUPREME: A Multi-GPU Framework for Reproducible Image Unlearning Method Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00380)
*Petros Andreou,Jamie Lanyon,Axel Finke,Georgina Cosma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SUPREME：一个开源、多GPU分布式的机器“遗忘”（unlearning）评测与实验框架，方便在多随机种子下高效完成训练-遗忘-评估流程，并支持易扩展注册式组件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器遗忘需要在多随机种子、不同设置下重复训练与评估，单GPU流程耗时高、难以系统比较方法；现有图像分类遗忘框架多为单GPU，限制可扩展性与复现实验规模。

Method: 构建SUPREME框架：1) 基于注册表的可插拔设计，便于新增方法、指标、模型与场景；2) 多GPU分布式架构，兼容多种加速器与数值精度模式；3) 在Pins人脸识别任务上，使用ResNet18与ViT，分别进行全类别与随机样本遗忘，跨10个随机种子进行演示与验证。

Result: 实现了跨多GPU的端到端训练-遗忘-评估流程，在Pins人脸识别上成功运行多种模型与场景，能够在十个种子下完成实验，展示出良好的可扩展性与效率（相较单GPU方案更快，细节未给定具体数值）。

Conclusion: SUPREME降低了机器遗忘研究的计算门槛，提供可扩展、可复现实验的平台；其多GPU与注册式设计便于社区快速集成与大规模评测。源码已开源于给定GitHub仓库。

Abstract: Machine unlearning removes the influence of specific training data from a trained model without retraining it from scratch. Evaluating an unlearning method requires repeating training, unlearning, and evaluation across multiple seeds, which is computationally expensive. To our knowledge, existing image classification unlearning frameworks run on a single GPU, which limits how many seeds can be evaluated in reasonable time. We introduce SUPREME, an open-source framework that distributes these stages across multiple GPUs. SUPREME makes three contributions: a registry-based design for adding new methods, metrics, models, and scenarios; a multi-GPU architecture supporting multiple accelerators and precision modes; and a demonstration on Pins Face Recognition using ResNet18 and ViT under full-class and random-sample unlearning across ten seeds. The framework is available at https://github.com/pedroandreou/supreme-unlearning.

### [41] [αDepth: Learning Single-Pass Soft Boundary Decomposition for Stereo Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00386)
*Xiang Zhang,Yang Zhang,Lukas Mehl,Karlis Martins Briedis,Markus Gross,Christopher Schroers*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出αDepth，一种分层表示，通过在软边界处同时估计分层颜色与深度，显著提升立体转换质量，避免背景渗漏与结构失真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层深度模型在软边界（如头发、散焦）处因前后景混合而产生深度对应歧义；传统抠图虽能提供不透明度用于分层建模，但在多目标复杂场景中效果不稳且常需人工交互。需要一种无需人工、可场景级推理、能准确处理软边界的分层深度表示。

Method: 提出αDepth与循环Alpha表示（CAR）。核心是在软边界处联合估计分层颜色与分层深度，化解颜色-深度混合歧义；以局部边界分解替代全局目标提取，使CAR可在多目标场景中高效推理，无需手工引导。

Result: 在大量评测中实现立体转换SOTA，显著消除软边界处的背景“出血”和结构畸变。

Conclusion: αDepth通过CAR将软边界建模为可分解的局部分层问题，实现无需人工的场景级分层推理，提升立体转换的保真度与稳健性。

Abstract: Accurately modeling soft boundaries, e.g., hair and defocus blur, is a fundamental challenge in stereo conversion due to the ambiguous blending of foreground and background. Existing depth models primarily predict single-layer depth, leading to ambiguity in depth correspondence at soft boundaries. While matting techniques can capture opacity for layered modeling, they often struggle in complex scenes with multiple targets and usually require user intervention. This paper introduces αDepth, a layered representation that decomposes soft boundaries for high-fidelity stereo conversion. Specifically, we first resolve mixed color and depth ambiguity by estimating layered color and depth values at soft boundaries. Considering complex multi-target scenes, we design a Circular Alpha Representation (CAR) that shifts the paradigm from global target extraction to local boundary decomposition. Unlike prior matting methods restricted to a single foreground/background, CAR enables efficient scene-level inference without manual guidance. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that αDepth achieves state-of-the-art performance in stereo conversion, eliminating background bleeding and structural distortions at soft boundaries.

### [42] [Zamba2-VL Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00390)
*Hassan Shapourian,Kasra Hejazi,Olabode M. Sule,Beren Millidge*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Zamba2-VL 是基于 Zamba2（Mamba2 SSM+少量共享 Transformer）的视觉语言模型家族，在多项图像理解/推理/OCR/指代/计数基准上与同规模开源 Transformer VLM（Molmo2、Qwen3-VL、InternVL3.5）相当，并显著超过现有 SSM/混合式 VLM（VL-Mamba、Cobra、mmMamba）。得益于近线性预填计算和小且近常数的循环状态，TTFT 约比 Transformer 基线低一个数量级，尤其在 1.2B/2.7B 小模型上优势明显。发布 1.2B、2.7B、7B 三个模型与推理代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 VLM 领域，Transformer 主导但在延迟与边缘部署上代价高；SSM 与混合架构有潜力提升效率但此前性能落后。作者希望在不牺牲精度的前提下，显著降低首 token 延迟与推理开销，特别面向小规模、端侧场景。

Method: 构建 Zamba2-VL：以 Zamba2 作为语言主干，融合 Mamba2 状态空间层与少量共享 Transformer 块；将视觉编码接入该混合主干，实现多任务（理解、推理、OCR、指代、计数）训练与评测；在相同参数规模下与主流 Transformer VLM 和既有 SSM/混合式 VLM 对比 TTFT 与精度。

Result: 在广泛基准上，精度与同规模顶级 Transformer 开源 VLM 持平或接近；显著超过以往 SSM/混合式 VLM。TTFT 较 Transformer 基线约低一个数量级，优势在 1.2B/2.7B 尺度最明显。发布 1.2B、2.7B、7B 模型与推理代码。

Conclusion: 混合 SSM+少量 Transformer 的 Zamba2-VL 可在保持 SOTA 级别精度的同时显著降低延迟，适合端侧与边缘部署；表明 SSM 主干结合少量 Transformer 是 VLM 高效推理的有效路径。

Abstract: We present Zamba2-VL, a suite of vision-language models built on Zamba2, a hybrid language-model architecture combining Mamba2 state-space layers with a small number of shared transformer blocks. Across a broad range of image understanding, reasoning, OCR, grounding, and counting benchmarks, Zamba2-VL is competitive with leading Transformer-based open-weight VLMs of comparable scale, including the Molmo2, Qwen3-VL, and InternVL3.5 families, and substantially outperforms prior SSM-based and hybrid VLMs such as VL-Mamba, Cobra, and mmMamba. Inheriting the near-linear prefill compute and small, near-constant recurrent state of its Zamba2 backbone, Zamba2-VL delivers roughly an order of magnitude lower time-to-first-token (TTFT) than these Transformer baselines at matched parameter scale, with the efficiency gap most pronounced at the smaller 1.2B and 2.7B scales most relevant to on-device and edge deployment. We release three models -- 1.2B, 2.7B, and 7B -- together with inference code at https://huggingface.co/collections/Zyphra/zamba2-vl.

### [43] [Rethinking Amortized Neural Representations for High-Resolution Terrain Elevation Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00404)
*Haoan Feng,Xin Xu,Leila De Floriani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出并评测面向地形高程数据的“摊销式隐式神经表示”（Amortized INR）方法，构建统一基准并发现跨领域性能差距。基于此，提出HUVR+SIREN：用可解析求导、平滑的SIREN坐标解码器替换HUVR的解码器，在不增加每瓦片存储、且解码更低成本的前提下，在高度与导数精度上达到最好，并在激进量化下仍保持质量。分析表明瓶颈主要在共享超网络结构，瓦片级负载已接近有效上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有INR对每个瓦片单独拟合与存储，难以扩展到大规模地形；摊销式表示虽能共享解码器，但方法多源自自然图像领域，未验证其在地形高度场上的适用性与设计取舍。需要受控基准来量化差距，并探索更适配地形的结构以兼顾高度与导数（坡度/曲率）保真、存储与解码效率。

Method: 1) 构建1 m/像素地形数据的受控基准与统一评测协议；2) 选择三种代表性摊销式方法（含一次前向超网络预测负载与短程优化恢复负载）进行对比；3) 观察跨域差距后，提出HUVR+SIREN：在HUVR框架中以SIREN作为坐标解码器，实现平滑且可解析求导的隐式表征；4) 系统地做消融与诊断，评估每瓦片负载大小、解码器结构、量化对性能与代价的影响。

Result: 在基准上，HUVR+SIREN在高度值与导数（坡度等）保真度上最佳；无需额外每瓦片存储，且解码成本更低；对激进的后训练量化高度鲁棒，几乎无质量损失；对比显示跨域差距显著，部分设计不易从自然图像直接迁移。

Conclusion: 平滑、可解析求导的SIREN解码器更适配地形高度场的连续性与导数需求，在摊销式框架下实现更优的精度—存储—算力折中。瓦片级负载容量已接近可用极限，主要改进空间在共享超网络的架构设计；HUVR+SIREN提供了紧凑、可量化的地形神经格式。

Abstract: Implicit neural representations (INRs) model a signal as a continuous coordinate-to-value function. For terrain elevation data, this supports analytic derivatives, arbitrary-resolution decoding, and a smooth surface model of the underlying heightfield. However, fitting and storing a separate INR for every tile does not scale to large terrain datasets. Amortized neural representations reduce this cost with a shared network: a new tile is mapped to a compact per-tile payload, and a shared decoder reconstructs the heightfield from it. Most such methods are hypernetworks that predict the payload in a single forward pass, while others recover it through a short per-tile optimization. These methods were developed primarily for natural images, and their suitability for terrain heightfields remains unclear. We introduce a controlled benchmark on a 1 m/pixel terrain dataset and evaluate three representative methods under a unified protocol. Observing a clear cross-domain gap, we propose HUVR+SIREN, a hypernetwork that adapts the strongest benchmarked method (HUVR) by replacing its coordinate decoder with a smooth, analytically differentiable one. It attains the best height and derivative fidelity on the benchmark with no additional per-tile storage and lower decode cost, and tolerates aggressive post-training quantization with negligible quality loss, giving a compact terrain neural format. Ablations and diagnostics further identify which design choices transfer to terrain and show that the per-tile bottleneck is already near its useful limit, leaving the remaining gap in the shared hypernetwork's architectural design.

</details>


### [44] [4D Radar Meets LiDAR and Camera: Cooperative Perception under Adverse Weather](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00416)
*Melih Yazgan,Iramm Hamdard,Qiyuan Wu,J. Marius Zoellner*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 将4D成像雷达引入多车协同感知，并用多智能体多模态的“多普勒引导空间注意力”进行融合；在恶劣天气中显著提升鲁棒性，雷达可替代或补充退化的激光雷达；发布含物理退化的雷达增强基准并在真实卡车场景有迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相机与激光雷达在雾、雨等恶劣天气下易退化，导致协同感知脆弱。需要一种对天气鲁棒的传感器与有效的跨车辆多模态融合策略，以保障全天候协同感知性能。

Method: 1) 将4D成像雷达纳入协同感知框架，分别构建两类骨干：a) 雷达-相机管线（雷达替代激光雷达）; b) 激光雷达-雷达管线（雷达补充激光雷达）。2) 设计“多普勒引导空间注意力”机制，利用雷达的速度/多普勒信息与空间先验，进行跨智能体的特征对齐与加权融合。3) 构建并发布含物理建模降级的雷达增强数据集与基准：OPV2V-R、Adver-City-R。4) 在仿真和真实数据（MAN TruckScenes）上验证。

Result: 在雾、雨等天气下取得明显鲁棒性提升：当激光雷达退化时，雷达替代可带来大幅性能增益；在雷达补充激光雷达的设置中也持续提升。方法在MAN TruckScenes上表现出从仿真到真实的迁移能力。

Conclusion: 4D成像雷达是实现全天候协同感知的关键鲁棒模态。结合多普勒引导的空间注意力，多车多模态融合在恶劣天气中依然可靠。数据集与代码已开源，促进后续研究。

Abstract: Cooperative perception is important for autonomous driving but remains fragile when cameras and LiDAR degrade in adverse weather. We address this challenge by integrating 4D imaging radar as a weather-robust modality into collaborative perception and introducing a Doppler-guided spatial attention mechanism for multi-agent fusion. Our approach extends two representative backbones: a radar-camera pipeline where radar substitutes LiDAR, and a LiDAR-radar pipeline where radar complements LiDAR. To support evaluation, we release radar-augmented benchmarks, OPV2V-R and Adver-City-R, with physics-based LiDAR degradation. Experiments show strong robustness gains in fog and rain, including substantial improvements when radar replaces degraded LiDAR. Additional validation on MAN TruckScenes demonstrates transfer beyond simulation. Overall, our results highlight 4D imaging radar as a robust modality for all-weather collaborative perception. Dataset and code are available at: https://url.fzi.de/SlimComm.

### [45] [Detect Before You Leap: Mirage Detection in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00435)
*Sayeed Shafayet Chowdhury,Md. Shaown Miah*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种在VLM作答前检测“海市蜃楼”(mirage)的预检测方法，通过对CLIP视觉编码器层内图像patch与问题文本的对齐轨迹建模，并与像素级空白/噪声检测、零样本域路由与VLM自评估集成，跨多域多模型显著降低误答为真（mirage）的发生率，三分类准确率约94.6–94.7%，mirage率<3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在证据缺失或不相关时仍会自信作答，尤其在医疗与文档VQA中风险极高，需要在回答前判断是否应作答以避免把无依据的答案当作基于图像的结论。

Method: 提出TC-LIA：对CLIP ViT-H/14各层图像patch token投影到最终CLIP嵌入空间，与问题嵌入计算相似度，得到跨层对齐轨迹；提取终层图文余弦相似度、后期层top-k patch-文本对齐、早-晚层增益、层间斜率等特征；并与像素统计的空白/噪声检测、零样本域路由、以及结构化VLM自评相结合形成集成判别器，实现“应答/弃答/其他”三分类。

Result: 在五个VQA领域、三种输入条件、十二个VLM骨干上评测，最佳系统三分类检测准确率约94.6–94.7%，mirage率低于3%，显著优于基线（mirage率21.7%–66.6%）。

Conclusion: 基于层内图文对齐轨迹的预发布mirage检测有效且模型无关，与多信号集成可稳健降低VLM的无依据作答风险，适用于高风险VQA场景。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) can produce confident visual answers even when the required visual evidence is missing, blank, or unrelated to the question. This failure mode, known as mirage (Asadi et al. 2026), is especially concerning in medical and document visual question answering, where plausible but visually ungrounded responses may be mistaken for image-based evidence. We study pre-release mirage detection: given an image-question pair, the goal is to determine whether a VLM should answer or abstain before producing a response. We propose Text-Conditioned Layer-wise Internal Alignment (TC-LIA), a model-agnostic method that probes patch-token representations across the layers of a CLIP ViT-H/14 vision encoder. TC-LIA projects layer-wise image patch tokens into the final CLIP embedding space and measures their similarity to the question embedding, allowing the method to track whether question-relevant visual evidence emerges across vision layers. The resulting alignment trajectory is summarized using final image-text cosine similarity, late-layer top-k patch-text alignment, early-to-late gain, and layer-wise slope. These features are combined with pixel-statistic blank/noise detection, zero-shot domain routing, and structured VLM self-assessment in an ensemble. Across five VQA domains, three input conditions, and twelve VLM backbones, the best systems achieve approximately 94.6-94.7% three-class detection accuracy with mirage rates below 3%, while baseline mirage rates range from 21.7% to 66.6%.

</details>


### [46] [Physical Object Understanding with a Physically Controllable World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00439)
*Rahul Venkatesh,Klemen Kotar,Lilian Naing Chen,Wanhee Lee,Gia Ancone,Seungwoo Kim,Luca Thomas Wheeler,Jared Watrous,Honglin Chen,Daniel Bear,Stefan Stojanov,Daniel LK Yamins*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种可对任意视觉变量进行条件概率估计的自回归概率世界模型，从视频中学习物理结构、对象与相互作用，并用其进行多未来预测、对象与部件发现、3D操控和物理关系推理（如视觉叠叠乐）。

Method: 构建一类新的概率世界模型，将视觉场景的外观与动力学等变量统一在可对任意子集进行条件化的分布式表征上；通过自回归序列建模进行高效训练；用顺序推断生成多种可能未来，并基于不同未来之间的运动相关性自动分割出对象及其关节化子部件；在发现对象后，利用模型在3D中对对象进行操控；从模型中计算对象间的物理关系以支持任务（如Visual Jenga）。

Result: 模型能从视频中产生多模态的物理一致未来预测；无需显式监督即可发现对象与关节结构；可在3D中对对象进行受物理约束的操控；能推断物体间的相互作用关系，并在视觉叠叠乐等应用中展现出有效性。

Conclusion: 自回归训练的通用概率世界模型可在无监督/弱监督条件下从视频中涌现对象理解与物理推理能力，能够进行多未来预测、对象分解与操控，并显式提取物理关系，提示此类模型是通往强大视觉世界模型与物理智能的可行路径。

Abstract: A central challenge in visual intelligence is learning the physical structure of scenes from raw videos: how regions form objects and the laws that govern their interactions. Solving these tasks requires world models capable of inferring distributional states of the world from partial observations - capabilities that current architectures do not provide. We introduce a new class of probabilistic world models that support estimation of the probability of any visual variable, such as appearance and dynamics, conditioned on any other variables. Here, we identify that these models can be trained efficiently with autoregressive sequence modeling, yielding world models from which rich object understanding emerges. First, we demonstrate that our model captures the physical laws governing how objects move by generating multiple plausible future states of the world through sequential inference. Then, by analyzing motion correlations across these futures, we extract objects and articulated object subparts. Having discovered these objects, we show that our world model can manipulate them in 3D. Finally, we demonstrate how physical relationships between objects can be computed from the world model, enabling applications such as Visual Jenga.

### [47] [Real-Time Physics Simulation with Dynamic Mesh-Gaussian Reconstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00444)
*Adrian Ramlal,John S. Zelek*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出将动态3D重建用于物理仿真时，需固定拓扑以高效碰撞检测，但领先方法（如 DG-Mesh）产生随时间变化的拓扑。作者提出双表示框架：物理用固定拓扑网格、渲染用高斯点渲染，并通过运行时顶点缓冲更新实现约4.65×加速。评估两种拓扑转换策略（时序对应跟踪、模板投影），结果显示均带来65–80%的几何退化，效果不如原生固定拓扑方法（MaGS）。结论：高质量重建与物理兼容拓扑是难以通过后处理兼得的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态重建结果常为可变拓扑，难以直接用于需要稳定网格结构的物理仿真（尤其碰撞检测）。现有高质量重建（DG-Mesh）与物理需求存在鸿沟，亟需探索是否可通过拓扑转换在不牺牲质量的情况下实现物理集成。

Method: 提出双表示框架：- 物理侧：使用固定拓扑网格以适配物理引擎；- 渲染侧：使用高斯splatting以保持外观质量。通过运行时更新顶点缓冲实现与动态重建同步。设计并实现两种拓扑转换策略：1) 基于时序对应的跟踪；2) 基于模板的投影。与原生固定拓扑方法 MaGS 在 DG-Mesh 数据集上对比。

Result: 双表示框架在速度上较变拓扑基线实现约4.65×加速。两种拓扑转换策略均导致显著几何质量损失（65–80%退化），总体表现不如 MaGS，即使 DG-Mesh 初始几何更优。

Conclusion: 单纯通过后处理将高质量变拓扑重建转为固定拓扑以适配物理仿真不可行，因目标冲突根本性存在。应发展“物理感知”的重建方法以在采集或优化阶段即考虑固定拓扑约束；所提双表示框架可与任意固定拓扑方法结合，实现实时仿真与渲染。

Abstract: Integrating dynamic 3D reconstructions into physics simulation requires fixed mesh topology for efficient collision detection, but state-of-the-art methods like DG-Mesh produce varying topology optimized for geometric quality. We investigate whether topology conversion can enable physics integration while preserving reconstruction fidelity. We propose a dual-representation framework combining fixed-topology meshes for physics with Gaussian splatting for rendering, achieving 4.65$\times$ speedup over varying-topology baselines through runtime vertex buffer updates. We evaluate two conversion strategies, temporal correspondence tracking and template-based projection, against native fixed-topology methods (MaGS) on the DG-Mesh dataset. Our evaluation reveals that both conversion approaches incur 65-80% geometric degradation, producing results inferior to MaGS despite DG-Mesh's superior initial quality. This demonstrates that high-quality reconstruction and physics-compatible topology represent fundamentally distinct objectives that cannot be reconciled through post-processing. Our findings inform future development of physics-aware reconstruction methods and our framework enables real-time simulation with any fixed-topology approach.

### [49] [GeoSAM-3D: Geodesic Prompt Propagation for Open-Vocabulary 3D Scene Segmentation from Monocular Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00447)
*Arun Sharma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GeoSAM-3D在仅用短单目视频的轻量设定下，实现“点击/命名一次 → 3D高斯场景上的跨帧与跨视角分割”传播。核心是基于重建后高斯质心图上的热核（图测地）距离来传播提示，而非3D欧氏近邻，从而更好保持曲面连贯并抑制相邻但不连通物体的泄漏。系统由冻结的图像/视频基础模型、单目3D Gaussian Splatting重建、可微图地质传播核、以及由SAM监督的特征头构成，并提出分离的评测协议（实现验证、图传播质量、泄漏控制、交互时延）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放词汇3D场景分割多依赖RGB-D、多视角标定或网格重建，代价高且使用门槛高。作者希望在更轻量、更易用的单目视频场景下，实现用户少量交互即可获得稳定的3D分割，同时解决传统3D欧氏近邻传播在曲面连续性与跨物体泄漏上的缺陷。

Method: 1) 用单目3D Gaussian Splatting对短视频重建高斯场；2) 在高斯质心构成的图上实现可微的热核（graph geodesic）传播，以热核距离扩散用户提示（点击/文本）；3) 结合冻结的图像与视频基础模型提取特征；4) 训练一个由Segment Anything掩码监督的特征头；5) 在代码库中提供geosam3d.propagate的数学实现与验证流程。

Result: 在给定代码库的验证中，图地质传播相较3D欧氏近邻更好保持曲面连续性并减少对近邻但不连通物体的泄漏；系统可在交互级时延下把单帧提示传播为跨帧、跨视角的3D掩码。

Conclusion: 以图测地热核为核心的提示传播在单目重建的高斯场景上有效，实现了轻量的开放词汇3D分割与较好的泄漏抑制和连续性；评测协议强调分离验证与交互性能，为后续改进（更强特征、更优图构建或核设计）提供了清晰路线。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary 3D scene segmentation usually assumes RGB-D video, calibrated multi-view imagery, or a reconstructed mesh. GeoSAM-3D studies a lighter setting: a user uploads a short monocular video, clicks or names an object in one frame, and receives a propagated 3D mask over a Gaussian scene. The implementation combines frozen image and video foundation models with a monocular 3D Gaussian Splatting reconstruction and a differentiable graph-geodesic propagation kernel over Gaussian centroids. The central design choice is to propagate prompts by heat-kernel distance on the reconstructed scene graph, rather than by Euclidean nearest neighbors in 3D. This preserves continuity around curved surfaces and reduces leakage across nearby but disconnected objects. This paper describes the repository state, the mathematical kernel implemented in geosam3d.propagate, the feature head trained from Segment Anything masks, and the validation already present in the codebase. The evaluation protocol separates implementation validation, graph propagation quality, leakage control, and interactive latency.

### [50] [Optimizing 3D Gaussian Splatting via Point Cloud Upsampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00450)
*Adrian Ramlal,Yan Song Hu,John S. Zelek*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文探讨如何通过改进初始点云来提升3D Gaussian Splatting（3DGS）重建质量，系统比较多种点云上采样方法并提出深度引导的点提升策略；实验表明不同方法在不同场景下各有所长，并给出选型建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS的重建质量高度依赖初始种子点的分布与密度，但现有流程多依赖稀疏/不均匀的SfM点或简单初始化，导致在纹理缺失或复杂几何处表现不稳。作者希望系统性研究不同上采样策略对初始化的影响，并提出能保持几何一致性的改进方案。

Method: 评估五类上采样/重建策略：线性插值、三角插值、样条曲面重建、移动最小二乘（MLS）曲面拟合、基于Voronoi的点生成；并提出利用深度图的“深度引导点提升”，在与SfM几何一致的约束下生成几何感知的点。于Mip-NeRF360与Replica数据集做大量实验，比较不同场景中的3DGS最终重建质量。

Result: 整体上，所有方法均可不同程度提升3DGS质量；曲面重建类方法在有机、细节丰富场景更优；简单插值在以分段平滑几何为主的场景更合适；深度引导方法能在全局范围（特别是低纹理区域）补充几何一致的点，显示出良好潜力。

Conclusion: 点云初始化显著影响3DGS重建；应依据场景特性与算力选择上采样策略：复杂有机场景优先用曲面重建，规整平滑场景可用简单插值；深度引导方法作为通用补充能增强纹理贫乏区域。研究为3DGS初始化提供了实践性指导与经验法则。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) is a technique for creating and rendering 3D scenes, however its performance depends heavily on the quality of initial seed points. To improve 3DGS initialization, this study presents and evaluates several point cloud upsampling approaches: linear interpolation, triangular interpolation, spline-based surface reconstruction, moving least squares surface fitting, and Voronoi-based point generation. Additionally, this research introduces a depth-guided point lifting method that leverages depth maps to maintain geometric consistency with Structure-from-Motion (SfM) reconstructions. Through extensive experiments on the Mip-NeRF360 and Replica datasets, the proposed methods demonstrate improvements in reconstruction quality across diverse scene types. Results indicate that different upsampling strategies excel in different scenarios: surface reconstruction methods perform better with organic, detailed scenes, while simpler interpolation approaches are more suited for scenes dominated by piecewise-smooth geometries. In comparison, the depth-guided approach shows promise for adding geometry-aware points across the entire scene, importantly in texture-less regions. These findings, which provide preliminary practical guidelines for selecting appropriate upsampling methods based on scene characteristics and computational constraints, advances the understanding of how point cloud initialization affects 3DGS quality.

### [51] [Beyond Static Gaussians: An Empirical Investigation of Architectural Paradigms for Dynamic 3D Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00452)
*Adrian Ramlal,John S. Zelek*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文综述了动态3D高斯溅射(3DGS)在重建动态场景中的两大范式，并在D-NeRF基准上比较其质量、速度与模型规模的权衡。结论：结构引导法更高保真更紧凑；高斯中心法更快可实时但质量波动大且可能更占存储。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态场景重建中方法众多且设计各异，社区缺乏系统性对比来理解在重建质量、渲染速度和模型规模上的取舍。本研究旨在为研究与应用选型提供实证与分类框架。

Method: 将动态3DGS方法分为两类：(1)结构引导：借助变形场、规范空间、网格等辅助结构表征时间变化；(2)高斯中心：直接在高斯原语中编码时间(连续函数或4D表示)。选取代表方法并在D-NeRF基准上统一评测，比较重建精度、渲染速度、模型大小与稳定性。

Result: 结构引导方法在重建保真度更高、模型更紧凑；高斯中心方法渲染显著更快，能达实时，但质量方差更大并可能带来较大的存储开销。

Conclusion: 动态3DGS存在核心权衡：质量/紧凑性 vs. 渲染速度。结构引导适合追求高保真与模型小型化的场景；高斯中心适合实时渲染需求。该结论为后续方法设计与应用部署提供方向指引。

Abstract: Dynamic scene reconstruction via 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has emerged as a compelling approach for representing evolving environments, yet understanding trade-offs between methodologies remains crucial. This paper presents a comprehensive analysis of dynamic 3DGS methods, categorizing them into two paradigms: structure-guided methods employing auxiliary representations (deformation fields, canonical spaces, grids) to model temporal changes, and gaussian-centric methods encoding dynamics directly into primitives via continuous functions or 4D representations. We evaluate representative methods from both paradigms on the D-NeRF benchmark. Our findings reveal that structure-guided methods achieve superior reconstruction fidelity and compact model sizes, while gaussian-centric approaches demonstrate significantly higher rendering speeds enabling real-time performance, though with greater quality variability and potentially substantial storage overhead. This analysis highlights a fundamental trade-off between reconstruction quality/compactness versus rendering speed, providing insights to guide future research and application development in dynamic scene reconstruction.

### [52] [An explainable hierarchical self attention-based approach for tremor detection in the time domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00461)
*Timothy Odonga,Jeanne M. Powell,Mark Saad,Richa Tripathi,Christine D. Esper,Stewart A. Factor,Hyeokhyen Kwon,J. Lucas Mckay*

TL;DR: 提出一个可解释的两阶段时域层级框架，用3D运动学时间序列端到端学习并在试次层面判别震颤；虽然平均F1=0.765不及频域SOTA(0.909)，但预处理少、具可解释性（注意力与Grad-CAM揭示时域与解剖学特征）。

Method: 两阶段层级模型：第一阶段以深度CNN+LSTM从短且不重叠的时域片段中学习局部震颤表征；第二阶段用Vision Transformer建模片段特征的长程时序依赖，实现试次（会话）级分类。使用3D运动学标记器数据，跨九个身体部位评估；采用注意力权重与Grad-CAM进行事后解释。

Conclusion: 以时域端到端学习进行震颤检测可行，能减少对专家频域特征的依赖并提供可解释性；尽管性能未达SOTA，但作为概念验证展示了跨解剖部位建模与可解释分析的潜力，未来可通过模型改进与数据扩充弥补性能差距。

Abstract: Tremor is a common movement disorder associated with conditions like Parkinson's disease and Essential tremor, traditionally diagnosed through expert clinician assessment. Current automated detection methods rely on frequency-domain features informed by clinical expertise. In this work, we present an explainable, two-stage hierarchical framework for tremor detection in the time domain that learns tremor patterns directly from 3D kinematic marker time-series data across entire tremor-provoking trials. Our framework combined a deep convolutional and long short-term memory network to learn tremor representations from short, discrete, non-overlapping time segments of kinematic time series data from trials, which are then processed by a vision transformer that models their long-term temporal dynamics of time segment features for trial (session) level classification. Evaluated across nine body parts, the framework achieved F1-scores of 0.594 - 0.947 depending on body parts (average: 0.765), falling short of the frequency-domain state-of-the-art performance (0.909) while requiring minimal preprocessing. Attention weights and gradient-based class activation maps (Grad-CAM) identified time-domain features of tremor across body parts. This proof of concept demonstrated the feasibility of data-driven time-domain modeling for tremor detection across anatomically diverse body parts, while reducing reliance on expert-engineered spectral features and providing posthoc interpretability of temporal and anatomical patterns of tremor.

### [53] [MUSCLE-NET: Predicted-Multiscale-Aware Network for Pedestrian Trajectory Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00471)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建MUSCLE-Net，包括两大模块：1) MMFE多尺度多模态特征提取：多尺度表示+模态感知重标定+方向性跨模态融合，将边框、速度、姿态对齐为语义一致表征；2) MEHP多尺度增强层级预测：以概率式粗预测器产生先验，进行尺度对齐融合与逐级细化，依据预测自适应选择尺度相关线索以抑制漂移。

Result: 在JAAD与PIE基准上取得与当前SOTA相当或更优的表现，带来稳定、持续的性能增益。

Conclusion: 融合多模态与多尺度、并在预测过程中自适应选择尺度信息，可显著提升不同行为与尺度下的行人轨迹预测精度与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Accurate pedestrian trajectory prediction is essential for safe navigation in autonomous driving and intelligent transportation systems. Despite substantial progress made by recent methods, most existing approaches are limited in fully exploiting diverse observations and often overlook the scale dependency of future motion, treating multiscale features uniformly regardless of underlying motion dynamics. This limits their robustness across diverse pedestrian behaviors. To address these challenges, we propose a Predicted-MUltiSCale-Aware Network (MUSCLE-NET) for Pedestrian Trajectory Forecasting that integrates complementary multimodal cues with scale-adaptive prediction mechanisms. The proposed framework is built upon a Multiscale Multimodal Feature Extraction (MMFE) module, which combines multiscale representation, modality-aware recalibration, and directional cross-modal fusion to construct semantically aligned representations from bounding boxes, velocities, and pose information. Building on these features, a Multiscale Enhanced Hierarchical Prediction (MEHP) module performs prediction-aware future-motion refinement via a probabilistic coarse predictor, scale-aligned fusion, and progressive refinement, adaptively selecting scale-relevant cues to mitigate spatial drift. Extensive experiments on the JAAD and PIE benchmarks demonstrate that the proposed MUSCLE-Net achieves competitive performance and consistent gains compared with state-of-the-art trajectory prediction methods.

</details>

CodeCytos is designed to streamline the exploration of custom spatial cellular features and adapt to diverse research needs. We demonstrate its utility through case studies on four expert-curated datasets from distinct tissue types: frontal cortex, non-small-cell lung cancer, pancreas, and tonsil. We evaluate CodeCytos under a realistic minimal prompt setting, where bioscientists pose simple questions without task-specific instructions or contextual information about spatial cellular analysis, and benchmark multiple LLM backbones with strong coding capabilities. ### [56] [Pre-Deployment Robustness Stress Testing for CT Segmentation Systems Using Clinically Motivated Multi-Corruption Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00491)
*CholMin Kang,Jonghyun Chung,Amanpreet Kaurb,Nagesh Gulkotwarb,Arthi Sivasankaranb*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RAMP 是一种面向鲁棒性的CT分割数据增广框架，通过解剖约束的空间扰动、CT强度变换与随机多重腐败组合，在训练中模拟临床异质成像退化，从而显著缩小干净到受损图像的性能落差并提升受损图像Dice。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 RAMP（Robustness via Augmented Multi-corruption Pipeline）：在训练阶段联合三类增广——(1) 解剖学约束的空间扰动（保证形变与器官解剖合理）；(2) 针对CT的强度域变换（对比度、窗宽窗位、强度偏移等）；(3) 随机多腐败组合（stochastic composition），在一次样本上叠加多种退化；以此系统暴露模型于临床可置信的退化分布。

Result: 在两套评测中均获最强受损图像表现与最小鲁棒性缺口：五器官噪声基准上，平均受损Dice由0.610→0.753，鲁棒性缺口由0.264→0.064，相较nnU-Net基线；在 Abdomen1K 上，平均受损Dice由0.633→0.789，缺口由0.290→0.070。尽管洁净图像Dice非最佳，但在严重退化下显著避免分割崩溃。

Conclusion: 多腐败增广是一种简便的部署前策略，可在临床异质环境中提升CT分割系统的可靠性，优先优化“最坏情况”稳健性而非仅追求洁净集精度。

Abstract: Deep learning-based CT segmentation systems often achieve high accuracy on clean benchmark images, but their performance may degrade under heterogeneous clinical imaging conditions such as noise, resolution loss, contrast variation, intensity shift, and artifacts. This instability can limit reliable deployment in real-world medical imaging workflows.
  We propose Robustness via Augmented Multi-corruption Pipeline (RAMP), a robustness-oriented augmentation framework for CT segmentation. RAMP combines anatomically constrained spatial perturbations, CT intensity transformations, and stochastic multi-corruption composition to expose models to clinically plausible image degradation during training.
  Across two CT segmentation evaluation settings, RAMP achieved the strongest corrupted-image performance and the smallest clean-to-corrupted robustness gap. In the five-organ noisy evaluation benchmark, RAMP improved mean corrupted Dice from 0.610 to 0.753 and reduced the robustness gap from 0.264 to 0.064 compared with the nnU-Net baseline. In Abdomen1K, RAMP improved mean corrupted Dice from 0.633 to 0.789 and reduced the robustness gap from 0.290 to 0.070. Although RAMP did not achieve the highest clean-image Dice, it substantially mitigated worst-case segmentation collapse under severe image degradation.
  These results suggest that multi-corruption augmentation can serve as a practical pre-deployment strategy for improving the reliability of CT segmentation systems in heterogeneous clinical environments.

### [57] [OptiWorld: Optimal Control for Video World Generation under Physical Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00499)
*Yu Yuan,Jianhao Yuan,Xijun Wang,Daiqing Li,Liu He,Lu Ling,Stanley H. Chan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出OptiWorld：在推理时将最优控制融入视频生成，使生成视频遵循更优、物理一致的轨迹。流程：提取紧凑任务状态→在受物理约束的流形上规划最优轨迹→按轨迹条件生成视频；适用于目标条件I2V、视频动力学编辑与反事实生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成更像“会动的渲染器”，缺乏对底层动力学的主动控制，常出现不安全、不平滑、低效或物理不一致的轨迹。需要把可解释、可约束的最优控制能力接入生成模型，以满足任务目标与物理约束。

Method: 推理阶段三步：1) 从视频/图像中抽取紧凑、与任务相关的世界状态表示；2) 将规划表述为连续流形上的几何优化，把3D几何与任务相关物理约束统一为“规划几何”，求解最优轨迹；3) 以该轨迹为条件渲染视频，使生成遵循规划的动力学。

Result: OptiWorld在多任务上生成具有更优动力学的视频：能实现目标条件图像转视频、视频动力学编辑、与反事实生成，展示出更平滑、安全、物理一致的轨迹与更可控的行为。

Conclusion: 通过在视频生成推理阶段加入最优控制层，并以几何化规划统一约束，OptiWorld使生成过程从“被动模拟”转为“主动控制”，显著提升可控性与物理一致性，并在多任务上展现通用潜力。

Abstract: Video generation models are becoming a scalable form of world models, but they mainly generate plausible motion rather than proactively control or optimize the underlying dynamics. As a result, an object in the generated video may follow trajectories that are unsafe, not smooth, inefficient, or physically inconsistent. In this work, we propose \textbf{OptiWorld}, a framework that brings classical optimal control into video generation at inference time. OptiWorld first extracts a compact, task-relevant world state, then plans an optimal trajectory under physical constraints, and finally renders the video conditioned on this trajectory. We formulate planning as a geometric problem on a continuous manifold, which converts 3D geometry and task-dependent physical constraints into a unified planning geometry. By adding this optimal-control layer, OptiWorld generates videos with preferable dynamics, demonstrating strong potential in multiple tasks including goal-conditioned image-to-video generation, video dynamics editing, and counterfactual generation.

### [58] [V-LynX: Token Interface Alignment for Video+X LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00508)
*Jungin Park,Jiyoung Lee,Kwanghoon Sohn*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发现视频大模型中的视觉token在内部形成“连续流形-Token接口”，据此提出V-LynX：无需重型模态编码器与成对监督，仅以轻量并行通路对齐注意力与统计分布，用非配对单模态数据将新模态接入，保持原模型冻结并兼容流形；在多项视听与多视角视频任务上达SOTA且高效。

Method: 提出V-LynX：在冻结视觉编码器的同时，新增一条轻量辅助通路，将新模态输入映射到与视频token同一内部流形。通过两类无配对对齐目标在单模态数据上训练：（1）注意力响应对齐，使新模态token引发的注意力模式与视频先验一致；（2）统计分布对齐，使新模态token的分布特性匹配视觉token。整个框架利用内化的token接口实现跨模态无配对对齐与可扩展集成。

Result: 在多项基准上取得SOTA与效率优势：音视频问答、3D推理、高帧率视频理解与多视角视频理解等任务均显著优于现有方法，同时保持较低计算/参数开销。

Conclusion: 视频LLM内部存在可复用的连续流形token接口。借助V-LynX，可用轻量、无配对训练将新模态无缝并入，既保留原模型能力又扩展多模态理解，并在多种视频相关任务上实现先进性能与高效率。

Abstract: This study introduces an intriguing phenomenon in Video LLMs: rather than merely translating frames into textual embeddings, Video LLMs establish a continuous manifold, token interface, allowing visual tokens to operate as standalone entities within the architecture. Exploiting this discovery, we propose V-LynX, a scalable framework that integrates novel modalities into Video LLMs by repurposing the internalized interface. Departing from conventional paradigms that necessitate heavy modality-specific encoders or paired supervision, V-LynX employs a lightweight auxiliary pathway in parallel with the frozen vision encoder. Our method integrates new sensory inputs with intrinsic video priors by aligning both attention responses and statistical distributions using unpaired unimodal data sets. This ensures manifold compatibility while preserving the integrity of the Video LLMs. Extensive benchmarks demonstrate that V-LynX achieves SOTA and efficiency across audio-visual QA, 3D reasoning, high-frame-rate, and multi-view video understanding. The code is available at https://github.com/park-jungin/lynx.

### [61] [ETC: Extreme Token Compression via Task-aware Visual Information Distillation in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00543)
*Yiling Gao,Hongchen Wei,Zhenzhong Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种极致令牌压缩（ETC）框架，用最小化任务损失为目标，在不显著牺牲性能的前提下大幅减少视觉令牌与KV缓存，甚至可压缩到单令牌仍保持较强效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率图像在VLM中会产生大量视觉令牌，导致推理计算与KV-cache开销巨大。需要在保持任务相关信息与性能的同时，极大地压缩视觉令牌表示。

Method: 从信息论与变分蒸馏出发：1）理论上证明最小化任务损失要求紧凑表示保留“面向指令的、与任务相关”的充分统计量；2）实践上利用文本-图像交互的跨注意力对视觉特征加权，近似潜在的指令感知预测统计量；3）通过变分信息蒸馏，使紧凑表示保留重构该统计量所需的关键信息，从而实现极致压缩（包括单令牌）。

Result: 在LLaVA-1.5-7B与Qwen3-VL-2B上验证，ETC在显著减少视觉令牌与KV-cache的情况下，依旧保持强任务性能；即使单令牌压缩也有效。

Conclusion: ETC提供了一种信息论驱动且可实践的令牌压缩方案，显著降低推理与缓存成本，同时维持VLM任务表现，为高分辨率视觉输入的高效推理提供通用路径。

Abstract: In Vision-Language Models (VLMs), high-resolution images produce a large number of visual tokens, resulting in high computational costs and KV-cache overhead during inference. To address this problem, we propose an Extreme Token Compression (ETC) framework that minimizes task loss when reducing the number of input tokens based on the principle of variational information distillation. Specifically, from an information-theoretic perspective, we show that minimizing task loss requires the compact representation to preserve the instruction-aware sufficient statistic of the task-relevant visual information for prediction. In practice, ETC leverages text-to-image cross-attention to weight the original visual features to approximate the latent instruction-aware predictive statistic. Moreover, ETC introduces a variational information distillation, enabling the compact representation to preserve the essential information to recover this predictive statistic. Experiments on LLaVA-1.5-7B and Qwen3-VL-2B show that ETC remains effective even under single-token compression, substantially reducing KV-cache overhead while retaining strong task performance.

</details>

Abstract: Concentrated Animal Feeding Operations (CAFOs) play an important role in agricultural production but are also associated with environmental, public health, and disease surveillance concerns. The resulting dataset contains more than 45,000 image patches spanning 20 states and four major CAFO categories. We benchmark a diverse set of convolutional, transformer-based, and vision-language models, demonstrating the value of refined annotations and curated negative samples for CAFO classification and generalization. CAFOSat provides a large-scale benchmark for advancing infrastructure-aware agricultural monitoring and CAFO mapping from high-resolution remote sensing imagery.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Visual grounding aims to locate image regions that correspond to natural language descriptions and is a key component of interpretable vision systems. Additionally, we explore an ensemble strategy based on majority voting across six diverse grounding pipelines, each with distinct capabilities. This multi-model framework improves robustness and significantly enhances localization accuracy.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) LatentFormer：使用可学习的二维token，并行生成受上下文调控的潜在视觉状态，每次更新直接锚定到原始图像特征，避免自回归累积误差；2) 连续空间RL：在嵌入空间直接优化潜在调制参数，提升潜表示质量；3) 训练流程：先知识蒸馏预训练，再以连续空间RL精调；4) 数据：构建DeepLatent-180K以适配潜变量视觉推理。

Abstract: The emerging paradigm of "thinking with images" embeds visual states into intermediate reasoning steps, defining a new frontier for Vision-Language Models. Existing approaches diverge along two lines. Tool-assisted methods apply explicit visual operations but suffer from high latency and restricted manipulation types. Latent reasoning methods autoregressively produce implicit visual states, but underperform tool-assisted methods, and their latent tokens fail to capture effective visual information. In this work, we propose DeepLatent, a parallel framework for latent visual reasoning. First, we introduce LatentFormer. It uses learnable 2D tokens to generate context-conditioned latent states in parallel, anchoring every visual update directly in the original image features. Second, we design a continuous-space reinforcement learning algorithm. It optimizes latent modulation parameters directly in the embedding space, significantly improving latent representation quality. The framework is trained via knowledge distillation followed by this continuous-space RL algorithm. Furthermore, we contribute DeepLatent-180K, a large-scale dataset tailored for latent visual reasoning. Extensive evaluations across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that DeepLatent achieves state-of-the-art performance.

### [65] [Decomposed On-Policy Distillation for Vision-Language Reasoning: Steering Gradients for Visual Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00564)
*Hee Suk Yoon,Eunseop Yoon,Jaehyun Jang,SooHwan Eom,Ji Woo Hong,Mark Hasegawa-Johnson,Qi Dai,Chong Luo,Chang D. Yoo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文将VLM蒸馏的损失拆解为语言先验与视觉对齐两部分，发现其梯度近乎正交；据此提出通过重定向更新向量以优先视觉子空间的VGS方法，在多种设定和基准上以极小开销显著提升视觉落地与整体推理表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有on-policy蒸馏为小型多模态推理模型提供稠密监督，但将损失当作单一目标，忽视了语言分布对齐与视觉落地的差异，可能导致优化走向对两者的次优折中；作者希望理解这种动态并提升视觉落地这一可能的主要瓶颈。

Method: 对VLM蒸馏目标进行数学分解：语言先验项与视觉落地项；分析两者梯度几乎正交。基于此，提出Visual Gradient Steering（VGS），在训练中动态重定向更新向量，提升在视觉子空间的分量，优先对齐视觉感知，同时保持语言对齐；实现为对梯度进行投影/重加权与方向校正，训练开销极小。

Result: 在多种蒸馏设定与复杂多模态基准上，VGS优于标准单一目标蒸馏，显著改善视觉落地指标，同时整体推理性能提升且训练额外开销很小。

Conclusion: VLM蒸馏目标包含语言与视觉两个几何近独立的子任务；单一优化会走向次优折中。通过VGS优先视觉梯度，可更好解决视觉落地瓶颈，在不增加显著成本的情况下提升多模态推理。

Abstract: While on-policy distillation offers dense supervision for training small reasoning models, its optimization dynamics in the multimodal domain remain under-explored. In this work, we challenge the standard monolithic view of Vision-Language Model (VLM) distillation by mathematically decomposing the loss into two distinct components: the language prior and visual grounding. Our analysis uncovers that gradient vectors for these components are nearly orthogonal, indicating that the objective of aligning with the teacher's language distribution is geometrically independent from the objective of matching its visual perception. Consequently, standard optimization passively follows a suboptimal compromise trajectory that implicitly balances the two objectives. Hypothesizing that visual grounding constitutes the primary bottleneck for vision-language reasoning, we introduce Visual Gradient Steering (VGS), a method that dynamically reorients the update vector to prioritize the visual subspace. Experimental results on multiple distillation settings and complex multimodal benchmarks demonstrate that VGS significantly outperforms the standard monolithic formulation of on-policy distillation, achieving superior grounding with minimal training overhead.

### [66] [Improving Visual Representation Alignment Generation with GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00583)
*Shentong Mo,Sukmin Yun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出VRPO，用强化学习式的“生成表征策略优化”替换静态对齐损失，在扩散Transformer中自适应对齐生成特征与预训练视觉表征，提升收敛和图像质量；在ImageNet-256上较REPA提升最高1.8 FID并将训练加速至2.3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散Transformer训练低效，因生成与判别表征对齐不足。REPA等方法用外部监督（固定余弦或对比损失）对齐噪声去噪特征与预训练编码器，但损失静态、缺乏任务自适应，难在保证生成质量的同时最大化判别一致性。

Method: 将表征对齐视为强化学习中的策略优化：以生成器内部扩散特征为“策略输出”，以与预训练视觉嵌入的一致性、生成保真度与感知质量为“奖励”，采用类似PPO的目标进行自适应更新。训练无缝嵌入SiT/DiT，几乎不增加计算；替换REPA的固定对齐损失为VRPO奖励驱动的优化。

Result: 在ImageNet 256×256上，VRPO-Alignment显著提升收敛速度与保真度：相较REPA，最高提升1.8的FID，并在相同计算预算下训练加速至2.3倍。

Conclusion: 将静态对齐转化为基于奖励的自适应优化可同时改进生成质量与语义一致性；VRPO与主流扩散Transformer兼容、计算开销可忽略，提供更快更好的训练收敛。

Abstract: Recent diffusion transformers have demonstrated strong image synthesis capabilities but remain inefficient to train due to weak alignment between generative and discriminative representations. While representation alignment frameworks such as REPA improve convergence by aligning noisy denoising features with pretrained visual encoders, their externally supervised alignment loss is static and lacks adaptivity during training and inference. Existing methods rely on fixed cosine alignment or contrastive objectives, which cannot dynamically balance representation consistency and generation quality, resulting in limited discriminative benefit and failing to optimize alignment in a task-adaptive manner. To address this, we propose VRPO, a reinforcement-based optimization strategy that replaces REPA's static alignment loss with a generative representation policy optimization objective. Instead of enforcing a fixed similarity constraint, VRPO treats representation alignment as a reward-guided process: the model receives adaptive rewards based on generation fidelity, perceptual quality, and semantic coherence between the diffusion features and pretrained visual embeddings. This formulation enables the generator to continuously refine its internal representations toward semantically meaningful directions while improving image quality. Our VRPO-driven training seamlessly integrates into diffusion transformers, introducing negligible computation cost and preserving full compatibility with SiT and DiT architectures. Extensive experiments on ImageNet-256x256 demonstrate that our VRPO-Alignment substantially enhances both convergence and fidelity, achieving up to +1.8 FID improvement and 2.3x faster training compared to REPA under identical compute budgets.

However, in clinical practice, physicians must often estimate long-term visual trajectories based only on early post-treatment findings, making reliable prognostication difficult. Although prior OCT-based learning approaches have largely focused on short-term response or single-endpoint prediction, modeling VA trajectories across multiple future time points from early longitudinal observations remains insufficiently explored. In this study, we assembled a real-world cohort of 188 anti-VEGF-treated DME patients with paired baseline and month-1 OCT scans, along with tabular OCT-derived biomarkers and non-imaging clinical variables. Using only these early data, we formulate a multi-horizon VA forecasting problem aimed at predicting visual outcomes at 3, 6, 12, 18, and 24 months, reflecting clinically meaningful follow-up intervals. We propose ReVA, a response-aware multimodal framework that integrates structural features from baseline and month-1 OCT with the tabular variables to capture baseline disease status and early treatment response. ReVA uses spatial attention to preserve localized prognostic imaging features and a dependency-aware tabular encoder to model interactions among clinical variables. These multimodal representations are fused to predict patient-specific long-term visual acuity trajectories. The proposed framework achieves MAE=0.1246, RMSE=0.1621, and R^2=0.6064 for 24-month VA prediction, with consistent performance across all forecast horizons. Abstract: Effective visual communication stems from the harmony of multiple design principles, such as readability, contrast, alignment, overlap, and coherence, which collectively govern clarity and intent of the communicator. While human designers reason holistically over these principles, machine agents typically condense them into a single heuristic score, offering limited interpretability and diagnostic precision. The benchmark comprises 100K perturbed training samples and 10K perturbed validation designs, each isolating a specific principle violation for controlled analysis of multimodal reasoning about design quality. We show that models like Qwen-2.5-VL and GPT-4o-mini are largely insensitive to targeted principle degradations, whereas GPT-4o exhibits global awareness without fine-grained disentanglement. Building on these insights, we propose a multi-scale evaluation framework that integrates lightweight scorers for quantitative assessment, instruction-tuned vision-language models for localised feedback, and prompt-based methods for global reasoning. Our framework provides interpretable explanations of design failures. Using these localised insights, we show targeted refinements that improve layout quality. Together, PRISM and our framework lay the foundation for interpretable design-literate multimodal reasoning systems.

Method: 提出ASAP框架：1）解剖感知知识注入：利用现成分割工具获得器官级先验，促使表示与解剖结构一致；2）语义自适应的选择性对齐：动态将报告中的句子级发现与局部体积区域对齐；3）语义自适应融合：在双模态掩码建模范式下，高效交互解剖感知视觉特征与落地的文本线索；并建立涵盖15数据集、22任务的标准化评测基准。

Result: 在异常分类、分割、预后预测、报告生成、词汇分类、跨模态检索、VQA等多任务和多数据集上取得SOTA；在有限监督与分布移位场景下提升尤为显著。

Conclusion: 将解剖先验与语义自适应对齐/融合纳入三维医学VLP可显著提升可迁移性与临床相关性；所构建的基准为系统评估医学体积VLP提供了标准协议。

Abstract: Learning transferable and interpretable representations from medical volumetric scans remains challenging due to complex anatomical structures and weak, heterogeneous supervision provided by radiology reports. In this paper, we propose Anatomy-aware Semantically-Adaptive Pre-training (ASAP), a principled vision-language pre-training framework for fine-grained medical volumetric representation learning from large-scale chest CT scans and their corresponding radiology reports. ASAP integrates three key components: (1) an anatomy-aware knowledge injection module that incorporates organ-level structural priors via off-the-shelf segmentation tool to encourage anatomically coherent representations; (2) a semantically-adaptive selective alignment mechanism that dynamically associates sentence-level findings with localized volumetric regions; and (3) a semantically-adaptive fusion module for effective interaction between anatomically informed visual features and grounded textual cues under dual-modal masked modeling paradigm. Beyond methodological contributions, we establish a comprehensive benchmark for medical volumetric vision-language pre-training on chest CT, covering 15 datasets and 22 downstream tasks spanning abnormality classification, segmentation, disease prognosis prediction, report generation, vocabulary classification, cross-modal retrieval and visual question answering. This benchmark provides standardized evaluation protocols to systematically assess representation quality under diverse clinical settings and data regimes. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ASAP consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance across tasks and datasets, with particularly pronounced gains under limited supervision and distribution shift, validating its effectiveness in learning transferable and clinically meaningful volumetric representations.

### [70] [FiSeR: Fine-Grained Source Representations for Cross-Domain AI Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00606)
*Shan Zhang,Yongxin He,Mingming Zhang,Huiwen Tian,Lei Ma*

Method: 提出层次化对比学习：同时优化两层目标——(i) 粗粒度：自然与合成之间的对比拉开两类间距；(ii) 细粒度：在合成图像内部基于生成器身份进行对比，保持并利用生成器区分性。训练于WildFake，主干学到更可迁移表征；推理用稳定的判别头。少样本自适应时冻结骨干，用每类10样本拟合SVM头。

Result: 跨域评测（Chameleon、AIGIBench、Community Forensics、GenImage）在与强基线DIRE相同设置下，平均AUROC提升+10.22。少样本适配下，平均提升AIGIBench +10.64、Chameleon +17.41，相比12个常用检测器。

Conclusion: 利用生成器层次结构进行分层对比学习，可在不依赖目标域标注的情况下显著增强跨域泛化；在仅需少量标注时，通过冻结骨干+SVM即可进一步提升表现。代码已开源（FiSeR）。

Abstract: Real-world synthetic image detectors often generalize poorly under domain shift despite strong in-domain performance. Using unsupervised UMAP projections, we find that natural and synthetic features remain partially separable on unseen datasets, yet performance still drops, suggesting that the classification head overfits to training-domain artifacts. Therefore, the key is to learn more transferable representations so that the decision criterion is more stable and robust to domain shifts. Based on the structural fact that synthetic images are produced by diverse generators, we propose a hierarchical contrastive learning framework that improves the separability between natural and synthetic images while preserving generator identity information. It jointly optimizes (i) a coarse contrastive objective between natural and synthetic images and (ii) a fine contrastive objective among synthetic images using generator identities. Trained on WildFake, our method achieves an average AUROC gain of +10.22 on cross-domain evaluation over Chameleon, AIGIBench, Community Forensics, and GenImage under the same settings as the strong baseline DIRE. For few-shot adaptation, we freeze the backbone and fit an SVM head on 10 labeled samples per class, improving AUROC by +10.64 on AIGIBench and +17.41 on Chameleon, averaged over 12 widely used detectors. Our code is publicly available at: https://github.com/heyongxin233/FiSeR.

To overcome this bottleneck, we propose FlowNar, a novel framework for scalable streaming video narration. *Yue Jiang,Xue Jiang,Lihua Zhang,Zhiqiang Wang,Yuhang Lu,Peng Wang,Bo Han,Feng Zheng,Dingkang Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评测多为单轮VQA，无法揭示多轮互动中因早期错误累积导致的语义崩塌与失去视觉锚定的问题，需要一个能刻画误差传播与对话动态的基准与对应缓解手段。

Method: 1) 构建MM-Snowball基准：针对对话场景设计可细粒度诊断的任务与度量，刻意诱发并跟踪幻觉滚雪球；2) 提出训练无关的CAVR：采用双机制——在表征层面刷新视觉锚定、在logit层面校正输出分布，使模型在冲突出现时重回视觉事实。

Result: 在MM-Snowball上，先进MLLM表现显著受挫，现有针对单轮VQA的缓解方法无效；CAVR在无需额外训练下取得最佳性能，显著减轻滚雪球效应。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) demonstrate remarkable visual understanding, yet their reliability in interactive settings is severely undermined by hallucination snowballing: a phenomenon where initial errors amplify across conversational turns, leading to a collapse in coherence. This failure reveals a fundamental vulnerability where models progressively neglect visual grounding in favor of over-relying on polluted textual history. Existing benchmarks are predominantly confined to single-turn VQA, which fail to capture the complex dynamics of error propagation in long-horizon interactions. To address this, we introduce MM-Snowball, the first benchmark for fine-grained diagnosis of hallucination snowballing within dialogues. Extensive evaluation shows that our benchmark poses a significant challenge even to advanced MLLMs and reveals the inefficacy of existing mitigation methods designed for single-turn VQA. To counteract this degradation, we propose Conflict-Aware Visual Rectification (CAVR). This training-free method mitigates snowballing through a synergistic dual-mechanism that refreshes visual grounding at the representation level and rectifies output distributions at the logit level, effectively re-anchoring the model to visual facts. Experiments demonstrate that CAVR achieves state-of-the-art performance, offering a promising path toward more reliable interactive AI. Data and code are available at: https://frenkie-chiang.github.io/MM-Snowball

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在公开ReMIND数据集（76例，153对ioUS/T2w与104对ioUS/FLAIR；按患者60/16训练/留出）上，对6种生成模型（Pix2Pix、SwinPix2Pix、CycleGAN、CUT、ResViT、SynDiff）分别在4种推理方案（2D、2.5D、2D+3D精炼、全3D）与2种目标（仅T2w；T2w+FLAIR多任务）下训练与评估，合计48个实验。采用影像保真度指标（SSIM、PSNR、MAE、LPIPS）、nnU-Net v2对肿瘤与切除腔分割的下游评估，以及按组织学分级与再手术进行亚组分析。

Conclusion: 评估MRI样合成时应优先报告或至少并列报告感知指标与下游任务指标，而非仅依赖全局SSIM；模型/推理选择应依据手术阶段、患者史与具体临床目标进行条件化。

Abstract: Intraoperative ultrasound (ioUS) is a versatile, cost-effective modality in brain tumour surgery, but its interpretation is difficult: acquisition planes are non-standard, artefacts are modality-specific, and its appearance differs markedly from the preoperative MRI on which surgical-planning tools, segmentation models and the surgeon's experience rely. Synthesising MRI-like images from ioUS could let this MRI-based infrastructure be reused intraoperatively without an extra scan. Most prior work evaluates a single architecture in isolation; to our knowledge, no benchmark has spanned architectural paradigms, inference regimes and downstream-task endpoints under a common protocol. We address this gap on the public ReMIND data set (76 patients; 153 paired ioUS/T2w and 104 paired ioUS/FLAIR studies; 60/16 patient-level train/held-out split). Image-fidelity metrics (SSIM, PSNR, MAE, LPIPS) were complemented by an nnU-Net v2 downstream segmentation evaluation (tumour and resection cavity) and by subgroup analyses by histological grade and reoperation. Perceptual and downstream-task metrics should therefore be reported alongside or in preference to global SSIM, and architecture choice conditioned on surgical phase, patient history and clinical objective.

### [75] [An Attribute-Based Measure of Video Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00640)
*Aditya Sarkar,Yi Li,Zihao Wang,Jiacheng Cheng,Sai Vidyaranya Nuthalapati,Aashu Singh,Shlok Kumar Mishra,David Jacobs,Nuno Vasconcelos*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VideoABC框架，用基于视频属性的非参数方法估计视频-问题对对视频LLM的“失败概率”作为复杂度；通过属性空间量化与两种量化器结合，并用心理物理学式合成视频填充格点，实现对分布内外样本的稳健复杂度估计；在低维属性下优于“LLM-as-judge”，且具有可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估视频LLM复杂度的方法要么依赖大模型判定、成本高且不稳，要么缺乏可解释性与对OOD样本的泛化。需要一种低成本、稳健、可解释的复杂度度量，能直接反映模型在特定视频-问题对上的失败风险。

Method: 将复杂度定义为失败概率。选取与复杂度相关的可解释视频属性（如场景复杂度、事件速度等），把参考视频投影到属性空间并进行量化：使用k-means量化覆盖分布内样本，提高精度；使用通用晶格量化覆盖分布外样本，保证泛化。通过受心理物理学“目标-干扰项”操控启发的合成视频生成流程，在训练时为晶格单元补足样本，计算各单元的期望ABC。测试时，将新样本投影到属性空间，查表输出其所在单元的期望复杂度作为估计。

Result: 在实验中，即便采用低维属性，VideoABC也能稳定估计复杂度，显著优于“video-LLM作为裁判”等基线，并以更低计算与实现复杂度达成。

Conclusion: VideoABC提供了低成本、可解释、对分布外样本稳健的复杂度估计工具，可用于分析基准的属性组成与难度来源，并为视频LLM评测与数据设计提供指导。

Abstract: A new framework for the estimation of the complexity posed by video-question pairs to video-LLMs, Video Attribute-Based Complexity (VideoABC), is proposed. Video complexity is defined as the probability of failure of a video-LLM for a given video-question pair. VideoABC is a non-parametric complexity measure, using a reference video dataset and a pre-defined vocabulary of video attributes informative of complexity, \eg the scene complexity or the speed of the video event informative of the question. In a training phase, reference videos are projected into the space of these attributes, which is then quantized. The expected ABC of each quantization cell is then computed. Given a new video and its projection into the attribute space, complexity is estimated by the expected ABC of the associated quantization cell. To enable the use of VideoABC with small reference video datasets, two quantizers are combined: a k-means quantizer that enables accurate complexity estimates for samples in the distribution of the reference dataset and a universal lattice quantizer that guarantees generalization to out-of-distribution samples. A synthetic video generation procedure, inspired by target-distractor manipulations of psychophysics studies, is proposed to populate the cells of the lattice quantizer during training, enabling the computation of their expected ABCs. Experimental results show that VideoABCis effective even with very low-dimensional attribute representations, substantially outperforming approaches like `video-LLM as judge' with much less complexity. Finally, the explainable nature of the VideoABC score, in terms of well-defined attributes, is shown to provide insights on how the attribute composition of benchmarks affects their complexity.

</details>


### [76] [Collaborative Few-Step Distillation and Low-Bit Quantization for Wan2.2 Dual-Expert Video Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00658)
*Jinyang Du,Shenghao Jin,Ziqian Xu,Ruihao Gong,Shiqiao Gu,Yang Yong,Jinyang Guo,Xianglong Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个面向部署的压缩方案：先用少步数分布匹配蒸馏，再进行低比特量化，并按双专家去噪路径分别校准高/低噪声分支与入口层，采用HiF4式表示提升动态范围；在蒸馏学生上校准量化，缓解分布失配。量化模型在同步数下接近全精度，且在8与20步平均优于原始全精度；20步性价比最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频扩散模型生成质量高但推理昂贵：步数多、参数常驻内存大，部署成本高。需要一种兼顾质量与效率的压缩与加速方法。

Method: 1) 采用分布匹配式少步蒸馏，将长步教师压缩为少步学生；2) 结合模型的双专家（高噪/低噪）去噪结构，分别对两条分支进行量化校准，并保护对量化敏感的入口层；3) 使用HiF4风格的低比特数值格式以覆盖更大动态范围；4) 在少步学生上进行量化校准而非在原始长步轨迹上，降低推理时的激活分布失配。

Result: 量化后的模型在相同步数下与全精度模型性能接近，并在8步与20步设置下平均超过原始全精度基线；整体显示出优良的质量-效率权衡，其中20步配置最佳。

Conclusion: 蒸馏与低比特量化的协同设计在视频扩散模型上有效：按双专家分支校准、保护关键层并采用HiF4表示，可在显著降低计算/存储成本的同时保持甚至超越全精度质量；20步为推荐的部署设置。

Abstract: Large video diffusion models achieve strong visual quality but remain expensive to deploy because each sample requires many denoising steps and a large resident parameter footprint. This paper studies a deployment-oriented compression pipeline for Wan2.2-T2V-A14B by combining few-step distribution-matching distillation with low-bit quantization. The pipeline follows the model's dual-expert denoising route, calibrates the high-noise and low-noise branches separately, protects sensitive entrance layers, and uses HiF4-style low-bit representation to improve dynamic-range coverage. Quantization is calibrated on the distilled few-step student rather than on the original long-step trajectory, reducing activation-distribution mismatch during inference. The proposed co-design keeps the quantized model close to the same-step full-precision model and surpasses the original full-precision baseline at 8 and 20 steps on average. The 20-step setting gives the best quality-efficiency trade-off in the tested configurations.

</details>

Abstract: This report presents TAP-JEPA, our runner-up submission to the EPIC-KITCHENS-100 (EK-100) Action Anticipation Challenge at EgoVis 2026. Instead of fine-tuning a large video backbone, TAP-JEPA builds a compact anticipation model on frozen V-JEPA 2.1 features: a ViT-G/384 encoder extracts visible pre-action tokens, the pre-trained latent predictor estimates near-future tokens from the observed context, and both token groups are fused by attentive probes with task-specific queries for verbs, nouns, and action pairs. For the final submission, we expand supervised training with the official training split and most of the validation split, reserving a small subset for sanity checks and qualitative inspection, and adopt a two-stage score fusion that first averages eight independently initialized probe replicas within each epoch and then merges candidates from epochs 12-20 with field-dependent weights. On the official open-testing leaderboard, our sunshinesky entry achieves 27.91 percent overall action Mean Top-5 Recall (MT5R), ranking second and only 0.04 percentage points behind the top score.

The results show a clear performance gap under external and cross-dataset evaluation, especially for benchmarks with different taxonomies, annotation protocols, spatial coverage, or temporal organization. Method: 形状先验驱动的两步补全：1) 实例选择模块（Instance Selection），在基线不产生proposal时也能识别前景点云并滤除背景；2) 基于对齐的点补全部件（Alignment-Based Point Completion），将前景点云在中心与朝向上对齐到形状原型，从原型中抽取点以填补缺失区域，实现结构一致的补全。方法嵌入单阶段全稀疏检测器推理流程。

Abstract: Single-stage fully sparse 3D object detectors rely on point clouds data to detect objects in autonomous driving scenarios. However, the sparsity and incompleteness of point clouds significantly limit the performance of 3D object detection. To address this issue, this paper proposes a point clouds completion method specifically designed for single-stage fully sparse detectors. The entire shape-prior-based completion process consists of two consecutive steps. In the first step, we design a novel Instance Selection module, which is capable of identifying point clouds corresponding to foreground objects even when the baseline model does not generate proposals, while effectively ignoring the point clouds of background regions. In the second step, we introduce a novel Alignment-Based Point Completion module, which aligns the point clouds of foreground objects with prototypes in terms of both their centers and orientations. Subsequently, points are selected from the prototype to fill in the missing parts of the foreground object. We evaluated our method on two single-stage fully sparse detectors using the KITTI dataset. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly improves the detection performance, confirming its effectiveness and generalizability.

Synthetic MRI generation can help address this imbalance by synthesizing target-modality volumes for dataset augmentation and controlled synthetic cohort creation. Abstract: Short-term anticipation in egocentric video requires more than recognizing the current scene: a system must infer which object the camera wearer will contact, which action will follow, and how soon the contact will happen. This report describes FROST-STA, our submission to the Ego4D Short-Term Object Interaction Anticipation (STA) Challenge at EgoVis 2026. For each query time, the model produces a ranked set of structured hypotheses containing an active-object box, noun label, verb label, time-to-contact (TTC), and confidence. FROST-STA builds on the V-JEPA 2.1 STA evaluation protocol, but adapts it to the challenge by using object-centric decoding, multi-head prediction, and a submission-oriented training and ensembling recipe. We keep the V-JEPA 2.1 ViT-G backbone fixed and extract two dense token streams: video tokens from a short clip resized to 384 pixels before the query, and image tokens from the last observed high-resolution frame. A compact alignment module, consisting of an attentive probe and frame-guided temporal pooling, maps the clip representation onto the spatial reference of the final frame before fusing it with image features. The fused maps are decoded by Faster R-CNN-style STA heads that estimate box offsets, nouns, verbs, TTC values, and interaction quality. For the final leaderboard entry, we train for 25 epochs with the official training split plus additional permitted validation annotations, and combine predictions across eight heads and checkpoints from epochs 15-25. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Diffusion Transformer，将Real-ISR建模为图像补全；设计解耦视觉先验注入：从LQ图像提取局部线索(恢复结构、支撑高频细节)与全局线索(引导整体生成、提升语义一致性)；对高度不确定区域，使用推理时agent在不改动模型参数下，依据LQ视觉证据自适应优化语义prompt。

Abstract: Real-world image super-resolution (Real-ISR) requires balancing structural fidelity to degraded observations with realistic detail synthesis. However, existing generative Real-ISR methods often rely on entangled conditioning mechanisms, leading to structural drift or semantically inconsistent details. To address this issue, we propose Visual In-Context Restoration (VICR), a Diffusion Transformer (DiT)-based framework that formulates Real-ISR as image completion. Specifically, we introduce a decoupled visual prior injection mechanism that derives local and global cues from the low-quality (LQ) image: local cues help recover image structures and support high-frequency detail synthesis, while global cues guide overall generation and promote semantic consistency. For ambiguous regions under severe degradation, VICR employs an inference-time agent to refine semantic prompts using visual evidence from the LQ input while keeping model parameters fixed. Experiments show that VICR achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple Real-ISR benchmarks with only 127M trainable parameters.

*Md Aminur Hossain,Ayush V. Patel,Nitant Dube,Biplab Banerjee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CR-JEPA用于跨模态遥感检索，采用模态特定stem+共享Transformer+JEPA预测目标，并用SIGR稳定投影，解耦同模态与跨模态检索头；在多数据集上验证，显著优于X-JEPA并以更少参数取得有竞争力同模态性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨模态遥感图像检索因成像物理、分辨率、光谱与外观差异大而难，且单一检索投影和单目标难以同时兼顾跨模态语义对齐与同模态邻域保持，需新的联合表征学习框架提升对齐稳定性与检索性能。

Method: 构建CR-JEPA：1) 模态特定stem提取初级特征；2) 共享Transformer主干进行联合表征；3) 采用JEPA式掩码预测目标，在同模态与跨模态间预测被遮蔽的潜在目标特征；4) 借鉴LeJEPA对原始检索投影施加Sketched Isotropic Gaussian Regularization以稳定嵌入、避免塌缩；5) 解耦检索头设计：统一同模态检索头与独立跨模态检索头分别优化。

Result: 在BEN-14K、CBRSIR_VS、DSRSID上评估；于BEN-14K上相较X-JEPA，S1→S2检索从61.23%提升至75.82%，S2→S1从63.73%提升至75.40%；同时以更少参数实现有竞争力的同模态检索。

Conclusion: CR-JEPA通过JEPA预测目标、SIGR正则与解耦检索头，有效实现跨模态语义对齐并保持同模态结构，显著提升跨模态检索性能且具参数效率，展示了在多遥感数据集上的广泛适用性。

Abstract: Cross-modal remote sensing image retrieval aims to retrieve semantically related scenes across heterogeneous sensing modalities. This remains challenging because paired observations may differ substantially in imaging physics, spatial resolution, spectral configuration, and visual appearance. Moreover, a single retrieval projection trained with one objective may be insufficient to jointly support cross-modal semantic alignment and same-modal neighbourhood preservation. We propose CR-JEPA, a Cross-modal Retrieval Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture for dual-modality remote sensing retrieval. The model uses modality-specific stems, a shared transformer trunk, and JEPA-style predictive objectives to estimate masked latent target features within and across modalities. Inspired by LeJEPA, we apply Sketched Isotropic Gaussian Regularization to raw retrieval projections to stabilize embeddings and mitigate collapse. CR-JEPA further employs a decoupled-head design with a unified retrieval head for same-modal retrieval and a cross-modal retrieval head for cross-modal search. We evaluate CR-JEPA on BEN-14K, CBRSIR_VS, and DSRSID. On BEN-14K, CR-JEPA improves S1 to S2 retrieval from 61.23% to 75.82% and S2 to S1 retrieval from 63.73% to 75.40% over X-JEPA, while also achieving competitive same-modal retrieval with fewer parameters.

</details>


### [85] [CASTLE2026 Team WDL Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00712)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CASTLE挑战要求从超过600小时、多视角的第一人称视频及其转录、辅助照片、人物/房间/时间等上下文中进行多模态长程推理，传统单模态或单一步推理方法难以支撑，需要一个能聚合多源证据并适配不同问题类型的有效系统。

Method: 构建基于Qwen的大语言模型多模态流水线：解析问题线索；检索相关ASR文本片段；附加辅助图像；从视频中采样候选帧；将问题路由到静态视觉、语音/文本、时间序列和混合四类，使用专用提示词；进行多次推理并以置信度加权投票；将结果转为Codabench官方格式。采用LoRA微调，并研究采样帧数量的影响。

Result: 消融实验显示：加入LoRA后得分由0.21提升至0.50；增加采样帧进一步升至0.58。最终系统在CASTLE Challenge @ EgoVis 2026中排名第一。

Conclusion: 证据感知的多模态路由与集成策略，结合LoRA微调和更丰富的帧采样，能显著提升长时第一人称视频问答性能，并在官方挑战中达到SOTA。

Abstract: The CASTLE Challenge @ EgoVis 2026 evaluates long-form egocentric video question answering over 600+ hours of multi-perspective recordings. Each four-choice question requires evidence from videos, transcripts, auxiliary photos, people, days, rooms, and temporal context. We propose an evidence-aware multimodal reasoning pipeline based on Qwen. Our system parses question hints, retrieves ASR chunks, attaches auxiliary images, samples candidate video frames, and routes questions into static visual, speech/text, temporal, and mixed types with specialized prompts. Multiple inference passes are aggregated by confidence-weighted voting and converted into the official Codabench format. In ablation, LoRA improves the score from 0.21 to 0.50, and more sampled frames further raise it to 0.58. Our final system ranks first in the CASTLE Challenge @ EgoVis 2026.

### [86] [Scaling Parallel Sequence Models to Foundation-Scale Vision Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00746)
*Yitong Jiang,Hongjun Wang,Collin McCarthy,Hanrong Ye,David Wehr,Xinhao Li,Qi Dou,Tianfan Xue,Ka Chun Cheung,Simon See,Wonmin Byeon,Ke Chen,Kai Han,Jinwei Gu,Hongxu Yin,Pavlo Molchanov,Jan Kautz,Sifei Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: C-GSPN提出以二维空间传播为核心的视觉基座编码器，通过高效CUDA实现、压缩潜空间传播块与双阶段蒸馏，将GSPN扩展到基金会规模，达到近线性复杂度与显著端到端加速，同时保持或超越ViT基线的精度与迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自注意力的二次复杂度限制了视觉基础模型在高分辨率和大规模预训练下的效率；现有亚二次方法多将图像展平成1D序列，削弱2D结构。GSPN能在2D网格上进行近线性传播，但原版实现效率低、难以作为基座模型。需要一种兼具2D结构保持、可扩展性与训练可行性的方案。

Method: 提出C-GSPN：1) 设计Warp-specialized的GSPN CUDA核，融合步进、共享内存tiling、合并内存访问与紧凑多通道传播，达90%+带宽利用率，较原GSPN快40–52倍；2) 采用带融合归一化的压缩潜空间传播块，将核级加速转化为块/模型级效率；3) 两阶段跨算子蒸馏，用注意力教师在无需从零大规模训练的情况下训练新架构。

Result: 在6亿图文对蒸馏下，C-GSPN以少15%参数匹配同构ViT基线；ADE20K分割提升+2.1%；高分辨率迁移所需额外数据显著减少；在2K分辨率下实现单次、无tiling推理，端到端块级速度提升约4倍。

Conclusion: C-GSPN将二维空间传播推进到基座规模，兼具近线性复杂度、硬件友好实现与跨算子蒸馏训练路线，在保持/提升精度的同时显著降低高分辨率与预训练成本，为替代自注意力的视觉编码器提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Vision foundation models are bottlenecked by the quadratic cost of self-attention, which limits usable resolution and increases the cost of large-scale pretraining. Subquadratic alternatives such as linear attention and state-space models reduce this cost, but often serialize images into 1D token streams and weaken the 2D spatial structure important for vision. Generalized Spatial Propagation Networks (GSPN) instead propagate context directly on the 2D grid through line-scan recurrences, achieving near-linear complexity without positional embeddings, but have seen little use as foundation-scale encoders.
  We present C-GSPN, a foundation-scale vision encoder based on 2D spatial propagation. C-GSPN makes the operator practical through three improvements: (1) a fast GSPN CUDA kernel that fuses per-step launches into a single warp-specialized implementation with shared-memory tiling, coalesced access, and a compact multi-channel propagation, reaching over 90% of peak memory bandwidth and running up to 40--52x faster than the original GSPN implementation; (2) a compressed latent-space propagation block with fused normalization, which turns kernel-level speed into block- and model-level efficiency; and (3) a two-stage cross-operator distillation recipe that trains the new architecture from an attention teacher without the cost of from-scratch foundation-scale training. Distilled with 600M image-text pairs, C-GSPN matches an isomorphic ViT baseline with 15% fewer parameters, improves ADE20K segmentation by +2.1%, transfers to high resolution with a fraction of the data needed from scratch, and delivers a 4x end-to-end block speedup at 2K with single-pass, tiling-free inference.

</details>


### [87] [SkyShield: Occupancy as a Safety Interface for Low-Altitude UAV Autonomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00747)
*Jie Gao,Jie Ma,Kaihui Lin,Kai Ye,Miaohui Zhang,Pingyang Dai,Liujuan Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机数据多为2D或3D框/地面传感器设定，不符合低空前视单目、机体6DoF动态外参与稀薄几何/遮挡/植被/城市杂波等安全关键特征；需要能直接评估“可进入/被占据”空间的基准与指标。

Result: 在该新设定下，传统mIoU可能掩盖安全风险；KAR-mIoU可揭示并放大关键风险。SkyOcc作为基线在语义占据上取得有竞争力表现，并更好保留碰撞关键结构（相对常规方法）。

Conclusion: SkyShield基准+KAR-mIoU指标+SkyOcc方法共同将“语义占据”确立为低空UAV自主的安全接口；数据集与代码将公开，期望推动低空城市飞行感知与安全评估研究。

Abstract: For low-altitude Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) autonomy, 3D spatial understanding is not merely a perception objective, but the safety interface between human instructions and physical flight. In human-scale urban airspace below 20 meters, thin geometry, occlusions, vegetation, and urban clutter define whether an aerial agent can safely enter the space ahead. However, existing UAV datasets mainly provide 2D annotations or 3D boxes, while driving-oriented occupancy benchmarks assume stable ground-level sensor rigs. Both miss the defining regime of low-altitude flight: a front-facing monocular camera observing occupied and free space from a moving aerial body with frame-wise changing 6-DoF pose and camera extrinsics. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{SkyShield}, to the best of our knowledge the first front-view monocular semantic occupancy benchmark for urban UAV flight below 20 meters. Built on CARLA, SkyShield contains 36K front-view UAV samples across diverse urban scenes and weather conditions, pairing each image with frame-wise 6-DoF UAV pose, frame-wise dynamic camera geometry, UAV states, and front-frustum semantic occupancy labels. We further propose \textbf{KAR-mIoU}, a UAV-centric and dynamics-aware metric that re-weights voxel-level evaluation by kinematic reachability and time-to-collision, revealing safety-critical risks hidden by conventional mIoU. To tackle this challenging new setting, we provide \textbf{SkyOcc}, a geometry-first monocular baseline that integrates frame-wise UAV attitude into projection, fuses temporal occupancy features, and applies safety-prior optimization to preserve sparse collision-critical structures. Together, SkyShield, KAR-mIoU, and SkyOcc establish occupancy as a safety interface for low-altitude aerial autonomy. Code and dataset will be released publicly.

### [88] [Head-Pose-Aware Visual Speech Recognition with FiLM Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00751)
*Matthew Kit Khinn Teng,Haibo Zhang,Takeshi Saitoh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HP-VSR-ResFiLM：在视觉语音识别中显式引入头部姿态，利用残差FiLM对CNN特征进行姿态调制，结合预训练NLLB完成音素到文本重建；在LRS2/LRS3上分别达成25.0%/33.2% WER，特别提升大偏航角样本的鲁棒性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 两阶段框架：1) 视觉编码阶段在2D CNN前端后加入姿态条件的残差FiLM模块，利用估计的头部姿态（如yaw/pitch/roll）对通道与特征逐点线性调制，得到姿态自适应的视觉表示；2) 语言阶段使用预训练NLLB将音素序列重建为文本。并做层级消融：单个FiLM与在第3/4层更深调制。

Conclusion: 显式的姿态感知特征调制是提升非受限场景VSR鲁棒性的有效且计算高效的方案，能缓解视角变化带来的表示不稳并改进整体识别性能。

Abstract: Visual Speech Recognition (VSR) aims to recognize speech from visual cues such as lip movements, but its performance is fundamentally limited by viseme ambiguity and pose-induced variations that introduce geometric distortions and occlusions. Existing approaches mainly rely on linguistic context or implicit invariance, leaving visual representations insufficiently robust under non-frontal views. In this work, we propose a pose-aware phoneme-level framework, termed HP-VSR-ResFiLM, that explicitly incorporates head-pose information into visual feature extraction. The proposed framework adopts a two-stage pipeline consisting of a pose-conditioned visual encoder in Stage 1 and a pretrained NLLB language model in Stage 2 for phoneme-to-text reconstruction. Specifically, Stage 1 incorporates a pose-conditioned residual Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) block after the 2D CNN frontend to adaptively refine visual representations using head-pose information. Experiments on LRS2 and LRS3 demonstrate that HP-VSR-ResFiLM achieves competitive performance under comparable training conditions, attaining word error rates (WER) of 25.0% and 33.2%, respectively, without relying on additional training data. Ablation studies further show that a single residual FiLM block consistently improves overall WER, while deeper modulation at Layers 3 and 4 provides larger gains for samples with yaw angles greater than 30° without degrading performance for smaller pose variations. These findings demonstrate that explicit pose-aware feature modulation offers an effective and computationally efficient solution for improving VSR robustness in unconstrained settings.
